Ensure UnicodeRange bits are properly set.

Check ID: <FontBakeryCheck:com.google.fonts/check/unicode_range_bits>
‚ö†Ô∏è output/Noto Looped Thai UI/unhinted/ttf/NotoLoopedThaiUI-Black.ttf
  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 0 "Basic Latin" should be 1 because cmap has 20 of the 128 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]

  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 1 "Latin-1 Supplement" should be 1 because cmap has 4 of the 128 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]

  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 6 "Combining Diacritical Marks" should be 1 because cmap has 1 of the 176 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]

  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 31 "General Punctuation" should be 1 because cmap has 17 of the 240 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]

  • ‚ö†Ô∏è WARN

    UnicodeRange bit 45 "Geometric Shapes" should be 1 because cmap has 1 of the 96 codepoints in this range. [code: bad-range-bit]
